<h2 class='a-header--2' id='hl_1'>Where Winds Meet Imperial Palace Guides</h2>
<p class='a-paragraph'>Version 1.7, The Imperial Palace released on May 28, 2026 featuring the long-awaited Kaifeng Imperial Palace region, along with numerous new bosses, quests, cosmetics, and more. Check out all our guides for the update:</p>

<p class='a-paragraph'><a class='a-btn' href='/games/Where-Winds-Meet/archives/602517' style='border-color: ; background-color: ; color: ;'><span>Version 1.7 The Imperial Palace Update</span></a></p>

<p class='a-paragraph'>The new update introduces over 50 Side Quests. These missions take you throughout the palace, introducing new NPCs, bosses, and activities.</p>
<h3 class='a-header--3' id='hm_2'>New Region: Imperial Palace</h3>
<table class='a-table a-table ' style=''>
  <tr>
    <td colspan=2 class="center"><img src='data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7' class='a-img lazy lazy-non-square' alt='The Imperial Palace' data-src='https://img.game8.co/4517090/2169eb3f322f3929a9841ca0c353a613.png/show' width='728' style='height: 0; padding-bottom: calc(px*409/728); padding-bottom: calc(min(100%,728px)*409/728);' /></td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
    <td colspan=2 class="center"><a class='a-link' href=/games/Where-Winds-Meet/archives/602736>Kaifeng Imperial Palace Exploration Guide</a></td>
  </tr>
</table>

<p class='a-paragraph'>The heavily guarded Imperial Palace of Kaifeng is now accessible to players at Level 32 who have completed <a class='a-link' href=/games/Where-Winds-Meet/archives/564658>Chapter 2</a> of the <a class='a-link' href=/games/Where-Winds-Meet/archives/563484>Main Story</a>. This new area features numerous NPCs, boss encounters, new Sentient Beings, fun activities and more!</p>

<p class='a-paragraph'><img src='data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7' class='a-img lazy lazy-non-square' alt='Palace Chronicle' data-src='https://img.game8.co/4516005/9cabe9dec216200be28d2e0a99b9c766.png/show' width='728' style='height: 0; padding-bottom: calc(px*382/728); padding-bottom: calc(min(100%,728px)*382/728);' /><br>On top of all the new content, there are numerous <a class='a-link' href=/games/Where-Winds-Meet/archives/568663>Events</a> and <a class='a-link' href=/games/Where-Winds-Meet/archives/564814>Cosmetics</a> added to the game. <h2 class='a-header--2' id='hl_2'>Where Winds Meet Latest News</h2>

<h3 class='a-header--3' id='hm_5'>The Hidden Mountain Expansion and Gauntlets on July 2026</h3>
<p class='a-paragraph'><div class='twitter-wrapper'><blockquote class='twitter-tweet' lang='en'><a href='https://twitter.com/WhereWindsMeet_/status/2063697501698273769?s=20'></a></blockquote><script defer src='https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js' charset='utf-8'></script></div><br>Along with the release on the Xbox platform, <b class='a-bold'>The Hidden Mountain Expansion</b> was announced to release on July 2026, featuring the Hidden Mountain region. Further details have yet to be announced. Moreover, the Martial Art path featuring the <a class='a-link' href=/games/Where-Winds-Meet/archives/602956>gauntlets</a> are expected to fully release on July 2026, as well.</p>

<p class='a-paragraph'><a class='a-btn' href='/games/Where-Winds-Meet/archives/604781' style='border-color: ; background-color: ; color: ;'><span>Hidden Mountain Announcement</span></a></p>
<h3 class='a-header--3' id='hm_6'>Currently Playable on Xbox!</h3>
<p class='a-paragraph'>As of June 8, 2026 (UTC+8), Where Winds Meet is now available in <b class='a-bold'>Xbox Series X|S, Xbox on PC, and Xbox Cloud Gaming</b>! The game has a crossplay feature that allows players to access the game in any of the available platforms of the game.</p>

<p class='a-paragraph'><a class='a-btn' href='/games/Where-Winds-Meet/archives/604756' style='border-color: ; background-color: ; color: ;'><span>Xbox Release Date</span></a></p>
<h3 class='a-header--3' id='hm_7'>Version 1.7: The Imperial Palace is Now Live!</h3>
<p class='a-paragraph'>On May 28, 2026 (UTC+8), the game had an update to include Version 1.7: The Imperial Palace, featuring the entire region of Kaifeng Imperial Palace. Apart from a new region, new quests, new features, new appearances, and new bosses were also introduced into the game.</p>

<p class='a-paragraph'><a class='a-btn' href='/games/Where-Winds-Meet/archives/602517' style='border-color: ; background-color: ; color: ;'><span>Version 1.7 The Imperial Palace Update</span></a></p>
